<s> savella i do arrest all present in the name of the pope's holiness <\s>
<s> you must to rome <\s>
<s> lucretia o not to rome <\s>
<s> indeed we are not guilty <\s>
<s> who dares talk of guilt <\s>
<s> my lord i am more innocent of parricide than is a child born fatherless ... dear mother your gentleness and patience are no shield for this keen judging world this two edged lie 115 which seems but is not <\s>
<s> will human laws rather will ye who are their ministers bar all access to retribution first and then when heaven doth interpose to do what ye neglect arming familiar things 120 to the redress of an unwonted crime make ye the victims who demanded it culprits <\s>
<s> tis ye are culprits <\s>
<s> that poor wretch who stands so pale and trembling and amazed if it be true he murdered cenci was 125 a sword in the right hand of justest god <\s>
<s> wherefore should i have wielded it <\s>
<s> unless the crimes which mortal tongue dare never name god therefore scruples to avenge <\s>
<s> savella you own that you desired his death <\s>
<s> beatrice it would have been 130 a crime no less than his if for one moment that fierce desire had faded in my heart <\s>
<s> tis true i did believe and hope and pray ay i even knew ... for god is wise and just that some strange sudden death hung over him <\s>
<s> 135 tis true that this did happen and most true there was no other rest for me on earth no other hope in heaven ... now what of this <\s>
<s> savella strange thoughts beget strange deeds and here are both i judge thee not <\s>
<s> beatrice and yet if you arrest me 140 you are the judge and executioner of that which is the life of life the breath of accusation kills an innocent name and leaves for lame acquittal the poor life which is a mask without it <\s>
<s> tis most false 145 that i am guilty of foul parricide although i must rejoice for justest cause that other hands have sent my father's soul to ask the mercy he denied to me <\s>
<s> now leave us free stain not a noble house 150 with vague surmises of rejected crime add to our sufferings and your own neglect no heavier sum let them have been enough leave us the wreck we have <\s>
<s> savella i dare not lady <\s>
<s> i pray that you prepare yourselves for rome 155 there the pope's further pleasure will be known <\s>
<s> lucretia o not to rome <\s>
<s> o take us not to rome <\s>
<s> beatrice why not to rome dear mother <\s>
<s> there as here our innocence is as an armed heel to trample accusation <\s>
<s> god is there 160 as here and with his shadow ever clothes the innocent the injured and the weak and such are we <\s>
<s> cheer up dear lady lean on me collect your wandering thoughts <\s>
<s> my lord as soon as you have taken some refreshment 165 and had all such examinations made upon the spot as may be necessary to the full understanding of this matter we shall be ready <\s>
<s> mother will you come <\s>
<s> they will bind us to the rack and wrest 170 self accusation from our agony <\s>
<s> will giacomo be there <\s>
<s> all present all confronted all demanding each from the other's countenance the thing which is in every heart <\s>
<s> 175 she faints and is borne out savella she faints an ill appearance this <\s>
<s> beatrice my lord she knows not yet the uses of the world <\s>
<s> she fears that power is as a beast which grasps and loosens not a snake whose look transmutes all things to guilt which is its nutriment <\s>
<s> 180 she cannot know how well the supine slaves of blind authority read the truth of things when written on a brow of guilelessness she sees not yet triumphant innocence stand at the judgement seat of mortal man 185 a judge and an accuser of the wrong which drags it there <\s>
<s> prepare yourself my lord our suite will join yours in the court below <\s>

<s> o that the hour when present had cast off 5 the mantle of its mystery and shown the ghastly form with which it now returns when its scared game is roused cheering the hounds of conscience to their prey <\s>
<s> it was a wicked thought a piteous deed 10 to kill an old and hoary headed father <\s>
<s> orsino it has turned out unluckily in truth <\s>

<s> my lord i am more innocent of parricide than is a child born fatherless ... dear mother your gentleness and patience are no shield for this keen judging world this two edged lie 115 which seems but is not <\s>
<s> will human laws rather will ye who are their ministers bar all access to retribution first and then when heaven doth interpose to do what ye neglect arming familiar things 120 to the redress of an unwonted crime make ye the victims who demanded it culprits <\s>

<s> savella you own that you desired his death <\s>
<s> beatrice it would have been 130 a crime no less than his if for one moment that fierce desire had faded in my heart <\s>
<s> tis true i did believe and hope and pray ay i even knew ... for god is wise and just that some strange sudden death hung over him <\s>
<s> 135 tis true that this did happen and most true there was no other rest for me on earth no other hope in heaven ... now what of this <\s>
<s> savella strange thoughts beget strange deeds and here are both i judge thee not <\s>
<s> beatrice and yet if you arrest me 140 you are the judge and executioner of that which is the life of life the breath of accusation kills an innocent name and leaves for lame acquittal the poor life which is a mask without it <\s>
<s> tis most false 145 that i am guilty of foul parricide although i must rejoice for justest cause that other hands have sent my father's soul to ask the mercy he denied to me <\s>
<s> now leave us free stain not a noble house 150 with vague surmises of rejected crime add to our sufferings and your own neglect no heavier sum let them have been enough leave us the wreck we have <\s>

<s> indeed we are not guilty <\s>
<s> who dares talk of guilt <\s>
<s> my lord i am more innocent of parricide than is a child born fatherless ... dear mother your gentleness and patience are no shield for this keen judging world this two edged lie 115 which seems but is not <\s>
<s> will human laws rather will ye who are their ministers bar all access to retribution first and then when heaven doth interpose to do what ye neglect arming familiar things 120 to the redress of an unwonted crime make ye the victims who demanded it culprits <\s>
<s> tis ye are culprits <\s>
<s> that poor wretch who stands so pale and trembling and amazed if it be true he murdered cenci was 125 a sword in the right hand of justest god <\s>
<s> wherefore should i have wielded it <\s>
<s> unless the crimes which mortal tongue dare never name god therefore scruples to avenge <\s>
<s> savella you own that you desired his death <\s>
<s> beatrice it would have been 130 a crime no less than his if for one moment that fierce desire had faded in my heart <\s>
<s> tis true i did believe and hope and pray ay i even knew ... for god is wise and just that some strange sudden death hung over him <\s>
<s> 135 tis true that this did happen and most true there was no other rest for me on earth no other hope in heaven ... now what of this <\s>
<s> savella strange thoughts beget strange deeds and here are both i judge thee not <\s>
<s> beatrice and yet if you arrest me 140 you are the judge and executioner of that which is the life of life the breath of accusation kills an innocent name and leaves for lame acquittal the poor life which is a mask without it <\s>
<s> tis most false 145 that i am guilty of foul parricide although i must rejoice for justest cause that other hands have sent my father's soul to ask the mercy he denied to me <\s>
<s> now leave us free stain not a noble house 150 with vague surmises of rejected crime add to our sufferings and your own neglect no heavier sum let them have been enough leave us the wreck we have <\s>

<s> tis most false 145 that i am guilty of foul parricide although i must rejoice for justest cause that other hands have sent my father's soul to ask the mercy he denied to me <\s>
<s> now leave us free stain not a noble house 150 with vague surmises of rejected crime add to our sufferings and your own neglect no heavier sum let them have been enough leave us the wreck we have <\s>

<s> 180 she cannot know how well the supine slaves of blind authority read the truth of things when written on a brow of guilelessness she sees not yet triumphant innocence stand at the judgement seat of mortal man 185 a judge and an accuser of the wrong which drags it there <\s>

<s> savella you own that you desired his death <\s>

<s> savella strange thoughts beget strange deeds and here are both i judge thee not <\s>
<s> beatrice and yet if you arrest me 140 you are the judge and executioner of that which is the life of life the breath of accusation kills an innocent name and leaves for lame acquittal the poor life which is a mask without it <\s>
<s> tis most false 145 that i am guilty of foul parricide although i must rejoice for justest cause that other hands have sent my father's soul to ask the mercy he denied to me <\s>

<s> lucretia o not to rome <\s>
<s> indeed we are not guilty <\s>
<s> who dares talk of guilt <\s>
<s> my lord i am more innocent of parricide than is a child born fatherless ... dear mother your gentleness and patience are no shield for this keen judging world this two edged lie 115 which seems but is not <\s>
<s> will human laws rather will ye who are their ministers bar all access to retribution first and then when heaven doth interpose to do what ye neglect arming familiar things 120 to the redress of an unwonted crime make ye the victims who demanded it culprits <\s>
<s> tis ye are culprits <\s>
<s> that poor wretch who stands so pale and trembling and amazed if it be true he murdered cenci was 125 a sword in the right hand of justest god <\s>
<s> wherefore should i have wielded it <\s>
<s> unless the crimes which mortal tongue dare never name god therefore scruples to avenge <\s>
<s> savella you own that you desired his death <\s>
<s> beatrice it would have been 130 a crime no less than his if for one moment that fierce desire had faded in my heart <\s>
<s> tis true i did believe and hope and pray ay i even knew ... for god is wise and just that some strange sudden death hung over him <\s>
<s> 135 tis true that this did happen and most true there was no other rest for me on earth no other hope in heaven ... now what of this <\s>
<s> savella strange thoughts beget strange deeds and here are both i judge thee not <\s>
<s> beatrice and yet if you arrest me 140 you are the judge and executioner of that which is the life of life the breath of accusation kills an innocent name and leaves for lame acquittal the poor life which is a mask without it <\s>
<s> tis most false 145 that i am guilty of foul parricide although i must rejoice for justest cause that other hands have sent my father's soul to ask the mercy he denied to me <\s>
<s> now leave us free stain not a noble house 150 with vague surmises of rejected crime add to our sufferings and your own neglect no heavier sum let them have been enough leave us the wreck we have <\s>
<s> savella i dare not lady <\s>
<s> i pray that you prepare yourselves for rome 155 there the pope's further pleasure will be known <\s>
<s> lucretia o not to rome <\s>
<s> o take us not to rome <\s>

<s> there as here our innocence is as an armed heel to trample accusation <\s>

<s> cheer up dear lady lean on me collect your wandering thoughts <\s>

<s> beatrice my lord she knows not yet the uses of the world <\s>
<s> she fears that power is as a beast which grasps and loosens not a snake whose look transmutes all things to guilt which is its nutriment <\s>
<s> 180 she cannot know how well the supine slaves of blind authority read the truth of things when written on a brow of guilelessness she sees not yet triumphant innocence stand at the judgement seat of mortal man 185 a judge and an accuser of the wrong which drags it there <\s>

<s> you must to rome <\s>

<s> indeed we are not guilty <\s>
<s> who dares talk of guilt <\s>
<s> my lord i am more innocent of parricide than is a child born fatherless ... dear mother your gentleness and patience are no shield for this keen judging world this two edged lie 115 which seems but is not <\s>
<s> will human laws rather will ye who are their ministers bar all access to retribution first and then when heaven doth interpose to do what ye neglect arming familiar things 120 to the redress of an unwonted crime make ye the victims who demanded it culprits <\s>
<s> tis ye are culprits <\s>
<s> that poor wretch who stands so pale and trembling and amazed if it be true he murdered cenci was 125 a sword in the right hand of justest god <\s>
<s> wherefore should i have wielded it <\s>
<s> unless the crimes which mortal tongue dare never name god therefore scruples to avenge <\s>
<s> savella you own that you desired his death <\s>
<s> beatrice it would have been 130 a crime no less than his if for one moment that fierce desire had faded in my heart <\s>
<s> tis true i did believe and hope and pray ay i even knew ... for god is wise and just that some strange sudden death hung over him <\s>
<s> 135 tis true that this did happen and most true there was no other rest for me on earth no other hope in heaven ... now what of this <\s>
<s> savella strange thoughts beget strange deeds and here are both i judge thee not <\s>
<s> beatrice and yet if you arrest me 140 you are the judge and executioner of that which is the life of life the breath of accusation kills an innocent name and leaves for lame acquittal the poor life which is a mask without it <\s>
<s> tis most false 145 that i am guilty of foul parricide although i must rejoice for justest cause that other hands have sent my father's soul to ask the mercy he denied to me <\s>
<s> now leave us free stain not a noble house 150 with vague surmises of rejected crime add to our sufferings and your own neglect no heavier sum let them have been enough leave us the wreck we have <\s>
<s> savella i dare not lady <\s>
<s> i pray that you prepare yourselves for rome 155 there the pope's further pleasure will be known <\s>
<s> lucretia o not to rome <\s>
<s> o take us not to rome <\s>
<s> beatrice why not to rome dear mother <\s>
<s> there as here our innocence is as an armed heel to trample accusation <\s>
<s> god is there 160 as here and with his shadow ever clothes the innocent the injured and the weak and such are we <\s>
<s> cheer up dear lady lean on me collect your wandering thoughts <\s>
<s> my lord as soon as you have taken some refreshment 165 and had all such examinations made upon the spot as may be necessary to the full understanding of this matter we shall be ready <\s>

<s> they will bind us to the rack and wrest 170 self accusation from our agony <\s>
<s> will giacomo be there <\s>
<s> all present all confronted all demanding each from the other's countenance the thing which is in every heart <\s>
<s> 175 she faints and is borne out savella she faints an ill appearance this <\s>
<s> beatrice my lord she knows not yet the uses of the world <\s>
<s> she fears that power is as a beast which grasps and loosens not a snake whose look transmutes all things to guilt which is its nutriment <\s>
<s> 180 she cannot know how well the supine slaves of blind authority read the truth of things when written on a brow of guilelessness she sees not yet triumphant innocence stand at the judgement seat of mortal man 185 a judge and an accuser of the wrong which drags it there <\s>
<s> prepare yourself my lord our suite will join yours in the court below <\s>

<s> scene 5.1 an apartment in orsino's palace <\s>
<s> enter orsino and giacomo <\s>
<s> giacomo do evil deeds thus quickly come to end <\s>
<s> o that the vain remorse which must chastise crimes done had but as loud a voice to warn as its keen sting is mortal to avenge <\s>
<s> o that the hour when present had cast off 5 the mantle of its mystery and shown the ghastly form with which it now returns when its scared game is roused cheering the hounds of conscience to their prey <\s>
<s> it was a wicked thought a piteous deed 10 to kill an old and hoary headed father <\s>
<s> orsino it has turned out unluckily in truth <\s>
<s> giacomo to violate the sacred doors of sleep to cheat kind nature of the placid death which she prepares for overwearied age 15 to drag from heaven an unrepentant soul which might have quenched in reconciling prayers a life of burning crimes ... <\s>

<s> beatrice mother what is done wisely is done well <\s>
<s> be bold 35 as thou art just <\s>
<s> tis like a truant child to fear that others know what thou hast done even from thine own strong consciousness and thus write on unsteady eyes and altered cheeks all thou wouldst hide <\s>
<s> be faithful to thyself 40 and fear no other witness but thy fear <\s>
<s> for if as cannot be some circumstance should rise in accusation we can blind suspicion with such cheap astonishment or overbear it with such guiltless pride 45 as murderers cannot feign <\s>
<s> the deed is done and what may follow now regards not me <\s>
<s> i am as universal as the light free as the earth surrounding air as firm as the world's centre <\s>

<s> savella strange thoughts beget strange deeds and here are both i judge thee not <\s>
<s> beatrice and yet if you arrest me 140 you are the judge and executioner of that which is the life of life the breath of accusation kills an innocent name and leaves for lame acquittal the poor life which is a mask without it <\s>
<s> tis most false 145 that i am guilty of foul parricide although i must rejoice for justest cause that other hands have sent my father's soul to ask the mercy he denied to me <\s>
<s> now leave us free stain not a noble house 150 with vague surmises of rejected crime add to our sufferings and your own neglect no heavier sum let them have been enough leave us the wreck we have <\s>

<s> 135 tis true that this did happen and most true there was no other rest for me on earth no other hope in heaven ... now what of this <\s>
<s> savella strange thoughts beget strange deeds and here are both i judge thee not <\s>
<s> beatrice and yet if you arrest me 140 you are the judge and executioner of that which is the life of life the breath of accusation kills an innocent name and leaves for lame acquittal the poor life which is a mask without it <\s>
<s> tis most false 145 that i am guilty of foul parricide although i must rejoice for justest cause that other hands have sent my father's soul to ask the mercy he denied to me <\s>
<s> now leave us free stain not a noble house 150 with vague surmises of rejected crime add to our sufferings and your own neglect no heavier sum let them have been enough leave us the wreck we have <\s>

<s> 180 she cannot know how well the supine slaves of blind authority read the truth of things when written on a brow of guilelessness she sees not yet triumphant innocence stand at the judgement seat of mortal man 185 a judge and an accuser of the wrong which drags it there <\s>

<s> will human laws rather will ye who are their ministers bar all access to retribution first and then when heaven doth interpose to do what ye neglect arming familiar things 120 to the redress of an unwonted crime make ye the victims who demanded it culprits <\s>
<s> tis ye are culprits <\s>
<s> that poor wretch who stands so pale and trembling and amazed if it be true he murdered cenci was 125 a sword in the right hand of justest god <\s>

<s> savella you own that you desired his death <\s>
<s> beatrice it would have been 130 a crime no less than his if for one moment that fierce desire had faded in my heart <\s>

<s> 135 tis true that this did happen and most true there was no other rest for me on earth no other hope in heaven ... now what of this <\s>
<s> savella strange thoughts beget strange deeds and here are both i judge thee not <\s>
<s> beatrice and yet if you arrest me 140 you are the judge and executioner of that which is the life of life the breath of accusation kills an innocent name and leaves for lame acquittal the poor life which is a mask without it <\s>
<s> tis most false 145 that i am guilty of foul parricide although i must rejoice for justest cause that other hands have sent my father's soul to ask the mercy he denied to me <\s>
<s> now leave us free stain not a noble house 150 with vague surmises of rejected crime add to our sufferings and your own neglect no heavier sum let them have been enough leave us the wreck we have <\s>

<s> savella can you name any who had an interest in his death <\s>
<s> i can name none who had not and those most who most lament that such a deed is done my mother and my sister and myself <\s>
<s> 70 savella tis strange <\s>
<s> there were clear marks of violence <\s>
<s> i found the old man's body in the moonlight hanging beneath the window of his chamber among the branches of a pine he could not have fallen there for all his limbs lay heaped 75 and effortless tis true there was no blood ... <\s>

<s> 95 lucretia her conduct throughout the scene is marked by extreme agitation ]: where was it found <\s>
<s> it should be orsino's hand <\s>
<s> it speaks of that strange horror which never yet found utterance but which made between that hapless child and her dead father a gulf of obscure hatred <\s>
<s> savella is it so <\s>
<s> 100 is it true lady that thy father did such outrages as to awaken in thee unfilial hate <\s>
<s> beatrice not hate twas more than hate this is most true yet wherefore question me <\s>
<s> savella there is a deed demanding question done 105 thou hast a secret which will answer not <\s>
<s> my lord your words are bold and rash <\s>
<s> savella i do arrest all present in the name of the pope's holiness <\s>
<s> you must to rome <\s>
<s> lucretia o not to rome <\s>
<s> indeed we are not guilty <\s>
<s> who dares talk of guilt <\s>
<s> my lord i am more innocent of parricide than is a child born fatherless ... dear mother your gentleness and patience are no shield for this keen judging world this two edged lie 115 which seems but is not <\s>
<s> will human laws rather will ye who are their ministers bar all access to retribution first and then when heaven doth interpose to do what ye neglect arming familiar things 120 to the redress of an unwonted crime make ye the victims who demanded it culprits <\s>
<s> tis ye are culprits <\s>
<s> that poor wretch who stands so pale and trembling and amazed if it be true he murdered cenci was 125 a sword in the right hand of justest god <\s>
<s> wherefore should i have wielded it <\s>
<s> unless the crimes which mortal tongue dare never name god therefore scruples to avenge <\s>
<s> savella you own that you desired his death <\s>
<s> beatrice it would have been 130 a crime no less than his if for one moment that fierce desire had faded in my heart <\s>
<s> tis true i did believe and hope and pray ay i even knew ... for god is wise and just that some strange sudden death hung over him <\s>
<s> 135 tis true that this did happen and most true there was no other rest for me on earth no other hope in heaven ... now what of this <\s>
<s> savella strange thoughts beget strange deeds and here are both i judge thee not <\s>
<s> beatrice and yet if you arrest me 140 you are the judge and executioner of that which is the life of life the breath of accusation kills an innocent name and leaves for lame acquittal the poor life which is a mask without it <\s>
<s> tis most false 145 that i am guilty of foul parricide although i must rejoice for justest cause that other hands have sent my father's soul to ask the mercy he denied to me <\s>
<s> now leave us free stain not a noble house 150 with vague surmises of rejected crime add to our sufferings and your own neglect no heavier sum let them have been enough leave us the wreck we have <\s>
<s> savella i dare not lady <\s>
<s> i pray that you prepare yourselves for rome 155 there the pope's further pleasure will be known <\s>
<s> lucretia o not to rome <\s>
<s> o take us not to rome <\s>
<s> beatrice why not to rome dear mother <\s>
<s> there as here our innocence is as an armed heel to trample accusation <\s>
<s> god is there 160 as here and with his shadow ever clothes the innocent the injured and the weak and such are we <\s>
<s> cheer up dear lady lean on me collect your wandering thoughts <\s>
<s> my lord as soon as you have taken some refreshment 165 and had all such examinations made upon the spot as may be necessary to the full understanding of this matter we shall be ready <\s>
<s> mother will you come <\s>
<s> they will bind us to the rack and wrest 170 self accusation from our agony <\s>
<s> will giacomo be there <\s>
<s> all present all confronted all demanding each from the other's countenance the thing which is in every heart <\s>
<s> 175 she faints and is borne out savella she faints an ill appearance this <\s>
<s> beatrice my lord she knows not yet the uses of the world <\s>
<s> she fears that power is as a beast which grasps and loosens not a snake whose look transmutes all things to guilt which is its nutriment <\s>
<s> 180 she cannot know how well the supine slaves of blind authority read the truth of things when written on a brow of guilelessness she sees not yet triumphant innocence stand at the judgement seat of mortal man 185 a judge and an accuser of the wrong which drags it there <\s>
<s> prepare yourself my lord our suite will join yours in the court below <\s>
<s> exeunt end of act 4 <\s>
<s> scene 5.1 an apartment in orsino's palace <\s>

<s> o that the vain remorse which must chastise crimes done had but as loud a voice to warn as its keen sting is mortal to avenge <\s>

<s> o that the hour when present had cast off 5 the mantle of its mystery and shown the ghastly form with which it now returns when its scared game is roused cheering the hounds of conscience to their prey <\s>
<s> it was a wicked thought a piteous deed 10 to kill an old and hoary headed father <\s>
<s> orsino it has turned out unluckily in truth <\s>

<s> my lord i am more innocent of parricide than is a child born fatherless ... dear mother your gentleness and patience are no shield for this keen judging world this two edged lie 115 which seems but is not <\s>
<s> will human laws rather will ye who are their ministers bar all access to retribution first and then when heaven doth interpose to do what ye neglect arming familiar things 120 to the redress of an unwonted crime make ye the victims who demanded it culprits <\s>

<s> savella you own that you desired his death <\s>
<s> beatrice it would have been 130 a crime no less than his if for one moment that fierce desire had faded in my heart <\s>
<s> tis true i did believe and hope and pray ay i even knew ... for god is wise and just that some strange sudden death hung over him <\s>
<s> 135 tis true that this did happen and most true there was no other rest for me on earth no other hope in heaven ... now what of this <\s>
<s> savella strange thoughts beget strange deeds and here are both i judge thee not <\s>
<s> beatrice and yet if you arrest me 140 you are the judge and executioner of that which is the life of life the breath of accusation kills an innocent name and leaves for lame acquittal the poor life which is a mask without it <\s>
<s> tis most false 145 that i am guilty of foul parricide although i must rejoice for justest cause that other hands have sent my father's soul to ask the mercy he denied to me <\s>
<s> now leave us free stain not a noble house 150 with vague surmises of rejected crime add to our sufferings and your own neglect no heavier sum let them have been enough leave us the wreck we have <\s>

<s> indeed we are not guilty <\s>
<s> who dares talk of guilt <\s>
<s> my lord i am more innocent of parricide than is a child born fatherless ... dear mother your gentleness and patience are no shield for this keen judging world this two edged lie 115 which seems but is not <\s>
<s> will human laws rather will ye who are their ministers bar all access to retribution first and then when heaven doth interpose to do what ye neglect arming familiar things 120 to the redress of an unwonted crime make ye the victims who demanded it culprits <\s>
<s> tis ye are culprits <\s>
<s> that poor wretch who stands so pale and trembling and amazed if it be true he murdered cenci was 125 a sword in the right hand of justest god <\s>
<s> wherefore should i have wielded it <\s>
<s> unless the crimes which mortal tongue dare never name god therefore scruples to avenge <\s>
<s> savella you own that you desired his death <\s>
<s> beatrice it would have been 130 a crime no less than his if for one moment that fierce desire had faded in my heart <\s>
<s> tis true i did believe and hope and pray ay i even knew ... for god is wise and just that some strange sudden death hung over him <\s>
<s> 135 tis true that this did happen and most true there was no other rest for me on earth no other hope in heaven ... now what of this <\s>
<s> savella strange thoughts beget strange deeds and here are both i judge thee not <\s>
<s> beatrice and yet if you arrest me 140 you are the judge and executioner of that which is the life of life the breath of accusation kills an innocent name and leaves for lame acquittal the poor life which is a mask without it <\s>
<s> tis most false 145 that i am guilty of foul parricide although i must rejoice for justest cause that other hands have sent my father's soul to ask the mercy he denied to me <\s>
<s> now leave us free stain not a noble house 150 with vague surmises of rejected crime add to our sufferings and your own neglect no heavier sum let them have been enough leave us the wreck we have <\s>

<s> tis most false 145 that i am guilty of foul parricide although i must rejoice for justest cause that other hands have sent my father's soul to ask the mercy he denied to me <\s>
<s> now leave us free stain not a noble house 150 with vague surmises of rejected crime add to our sufferings and your own neglect no heavier sum let them have been enough leave us the wreck we have <\s>

<s> 180 she cannot know how well the supine slaves of blind authority read the truth of things when written on a brow of guilelessness she sees not yet triumphant innocence stand at the judgement seat of mortal man 185 a judge and an accuser of the wrong which drags it there <\s>

<s> savella you own that you desired his death <\s>

<s> savella strange thoughts beget strange deeds and here are both i judge thee not <\s>
<s> beatrice and yet if you arrest me 140 you are the judge and executioner of that which is the life of life the breath of accusation kills an innocent name and leaves for lame acquittal the poor life which is a mask without it <\s>
<s> tis most false 145 that i am guilty of foul parricide although i must rejoice for justest cause that other hands have sent my father's soul to ask the mercy he denied to me <\s>

<s> lucretia o not to rome <\s>
<s> indeed we are not guilty <\s>
<s> who dares talk of guilt <\s>
<s> my lord i am more innocent of parricide than is a child born fatherless ... dear mother your gentleness and patience are no shield for this keen judging world this two edged lie 115 which seems but is not <\s>
<s> will human laws rather will ye who are their ministers bar all access to retribution first and then when heaven doth interpose to do what ye neglect arming familiar things 120 to the redress of an unwonted crime make ye the victims who demanded it culprits <\s>
<s> tis ye are culprits <\s>
<s> that poor wretch who stands so pale and trembling and amazed if it be true he murdered cenci was 125 a sword in the right hand of justest god <\s>
<s> wherefore should i have wielded it <\s>
<s> unless the crimes which mortal tongue dare never name god therefore scruples to avenge <\s>
<s> savella you own that you desired his death <\s>
<s> beatrice it would have been 130 a crime no less than his if for one moment that fierce desire had faded in my heart <\s>
<s> tis true i did believe and hope and pray ay i even knew ... for god is wise and just that some strange sudden death hung over him <\s>
<s> 135 tis true that this did happen and most true there was no other rest for me on earth no other hope in heaven ... now what of this <\s>
<s> savella strange thoughts beget strange deeds and here are both i judge thee not <\s>
<s> beatrice and yet if you arrest me 140 you are the judge and executioner of that which is the life of life the breath of accusation kills an innocent name and leaves for lame acquittal the poor life which is a mask without it <\s>
<s> tis most false 145 that i am guilty of foul parricide although i must rejoice for justest cause that other hands have sent my father's soul to ask the mercy he denied to me <\s>
<s> now leave us free stain not a noble house 150 with vague surmises of rejected crime add to our sufferings and your own neglect no heavier sum let them have been enough leave us the wreck we have <\s>
<s> savella i dare not lady <\s>
<s> i pray that you prepare yourselves for rome 155 there the pope's further pleasure will be known <\s>
<s> lucretia o not to rome <\s>
<s> o take us not to rome <\s>

<s> there as here our innocence is as an armed heel to trample accusation <\s>

<s> cheer up dear lady lean on me collect your wandering thoughts <\s>

<s> beatrice my lord she knows not yet the uses of the world <\s>
<s> she fears that power is as a beast which grasps and loosens not a snake whose look transmutes all things to guilt which is its nutriment <\s>
<s> 180 she cannot know how well the supine slaves of blind authority read the truth of things when written on a brow of guilelessness she sees not yet triumphant innocence stand at the judgement seat of mortal man 185 a judge and an accuser of the wrong which drags it there <\s>

<s> you must to rome <\s>

<s> indeed we are not guilty <\s>
<s> who dares talk of guilt <\s>
<s> my lord i am more innocent of parricide than is a child born fatherless ... dear mother your gentleness and patience are no shield for this keen judging world this two edged lie 115 which seems but is not <\s>
<s> will human laws rather will ye who are their ministers bar all access to retribution first and then when heaven doth interpose to do what ye neglect arming familiar things 120 to the redress of an unwonted crime make ye the victims who demanded it culprits <\s>
<s> tis ye are culprits <\s>
<s> that poor wretch who stands so pale and trembling and amazed if it be true he murdered cenci was 125 a sword in the right hand of justest god <\s>
<s> wherefore should i have wielded it <\s>
<s> unless the crimes which mortal tongue dare never name god therefore scruples to avenge <\s>
<s> savella you own that you desired his death <\s>
<s> beatrice it would have been 130 a crime no less than his if for one moment that fierce desire had faded in my heart <\s>
<s> tis true i did believe and hope and pray ay i even knew ... for god is wise and just that some strange sudden death hung over him <\s>
<s> 135 tis true that this did happen and most true there was no other rest for me on earth no other hope in heaven ... now what of this <\s>
<s> savella strange thoughts beget strange deeds and here are both i judge thee not <\s>
<s> beatrice and yet if you arrest me 140 you are the judge and executioner of that which is the life of life the breath of accusation kills an innocent name and leaves for lame acquittal the poor life which is a mask without it <\s>
<s> tis most false 145 that i am guilty of foul parricide although i must rejoice for justest cause that other hands have sent my father's soul to ask the mercy he denied to me <\s>
<s> now leave us free stain not a noble house 150 with vague surmises of rejected crime add to our sufferings and your own neglect no heavier sum let them have been enough leave us the wreck we have <\s>
<s> savella i dare not lady <\s>
<s> i pray that you prepare yourselves for rome 155 there the pope's further pleasure will be known <\s>
<s> lucretia o not to rome <\s>
<s> o take us not to rome <\s>
<s> beatrice why not to rome dear mother <\s>
<s> there as here our innocence is as an armed heel to trample accusation <\s>
<s> god is there 160 as here and with his shadow ever clothes the innocent the injured and the weak and such are we <\s>
<s> cheer up dear lady lean on me collect your wandering thoughts <\s>
<s> my lord as soon as you have taken some refreshment 165 and had all such examinations made upon the spot as may be necessary to the full understanding of this matter we shall be ready <\s>

<s> they will bind us to the rack and wrest 170 self accusation from our agony <\s>
<s> will giacomo be there <\s>
<s> all present all confronted all demanding each from the other's countenance the thing which is in every heart <\s>
<s> 175 she faints and is borne out savella she faints an ill appearance this <\s>
<s> beatrice my lord she knows not yet the uses of the world <\s>
<s> she fears that power is as a beast which grasps and loosens not a snake whose look transmutes all things to guilt which is its nutriment <\s>
<s> 180 she cannot know how well the supine slaves of blind authority read the truth of things when written on a brow of guilelessness she sees not yet triumphant innocence stand at the judgement seat of mortal man 185 a judge and an accuser of the wrong which drags it there <\s>
<s> prepare yourself my lord our suite will join yours in the court below <\s>

<s> scene 5.1 an apartment in orsino's palace <\s>
<s> enter orsino and giacomo <\s>
<s> giacomo do evil deeds thus quickly come to end <\s>
<s> o that the vain remorse which must chastise crimes done had but as loud a voice to warn as its keen sting is mortal to avenge <\s>
<s> o that the hour when present had cast off 5 the mantle of its mystery and shown the ghastly form with which it now returns when its scared game is roused cheering the hounds of conscience to their prey <\s>
<s> it was a wicked thought a piteous deed 10 to kill an old and hoary headed father <\s>
<s> orsino it has turned out unluckily in truth <\s>
<s> giacomo to violate the sacred doors of sleep to cheat kind nature of the placid death which she prepares for overwearied age 15 to drag from heaven an unrepentant soul which might have quenched in reconciling prayers a life of burning crimes ... <\s>

<s> beatrice mother what is done wisely is done well <\s>
<s> be bold 35 as thou art just <\s>
<s> tis like a truant child to fear that others know what thou hast done even from thine own strong consciousness and thus write on unsteady eyes and altered cheeks all thou wouldst hide <\s>
<s> be faithful to thyself 40 and fear no other witness but thy fear <\s>
<s> for if as cannot be some circumstance should rise in accusation we can blind suspicion with such cheap astonishment or overbear it with such guiltless pride 45 as murderers cannot feign <\s>
<s> the deed is done and what may follow now regards not me <\s>
<s> i am as universal as the light free as the earth surrounding air as firm as the world's centre <\s>

<s> savella strange thoughts beget strange deeds and here are both i judge thee not <\s>
<s> beatrice and yet if you arrest me 140 you are the judge and executioner of that which is the life of life the breath of accusation kills an innocent name and leaves for lame acquittal the poor life which is a mask without it <\s>
<s> tis most false 145 that i am guilty of foul parricide although i must rejoice for justest cause that other hands have sent my father's soul to ask the mercy he denied to me <\s>
<s> now leave us free stain not a noble house 150 with vague surmises of rejected crime add to our sufferings and your own neglect no heavier sum let them have been enough leave us the wreck we have <\s>

<s> 135 tis true that this did happen and most true there was no other rest for me on earth no other hope in heaven ... now what of this <\s>
<s> savella strange thoughts beget strange deeds and here are both i judge thee not <\s>
<s> beatrice and yet if you arrest me 140 you are the judge and executioner of that which is the life of life the breath of accusation kills an innocent name and leaves for lame acquittal the poor life which is a mask without it <\s>
<s> tis most false 145 that i am guilty of foul parricide although i must rejoice for justest cause that other hands have sent my father's soul to ask the mercy he denied to me <\s>
<s> now leave us free stain not a noble house 150 with vague surmises of rejected crime add to our sufferings and your own neglect no heavier sum let them have been enough leave us the wreck we have <\s>

<s> 180 she cannot know how well the supine slaves of blind authority read the truth of things when written on a brow of guilelessness she sees not yet triumphant innocence stand at the judgement seat of mortal man 185 a judge and an accuser of the wrong which drags it there <\s>

<s> will human laws rather will ye who are their ministers bar all access to retribution first and then when heaven doth interpose to do what ye neglect arming familiar things 120 to the redress of an unwonted crime make ye the victims who demanded it culprits <\s>
<s> tis ye are culprits <\s>
<s> that poor wretch who stands so pale and trembling and amazed if it be true he murdered cenci was 125 a sword in the right hand of justest god <\s>

<s> savella you own that you desired his death <\s>
<s> beatrice it would have been 130 a crime no less than his if for one moment that fierce desire had faded in my heart <\s>

<s> 135 tis true that this did happen and most true there was no other rest for me on earth no other hope in heaven ... now what of this <\s>
<s> savella strange thoughts beget strange deeds and here are both i judge thee not <\s>
<s> beatrice and yet if you arrest me 140 you are the judge and executioner of that which is the life of life the breath of accusation kills an innocent name and leaves for lame acquittal the poor life which is a mask without it <\s>
<s> tis most false 145 that i am guilty of foul parricide although i must rejoice for justest cause that other hands have sent my father's soul to ask the mercy he denied to me <\s>
<s> now leave us free stain not a noble house 150 with vague surmises of rejected crime add to our sufferings and your own neglect no heavier sum let them have been enough leave us the wreck we have <\s>

<s> savella can you name any who had an interest in his death <\s>
<s> i can name none who had not and those most who most lament that such a deed is done my mother and my sister and myself <\s>
<s> 70 savella tis strange <\s>
<s> there were clear marks of violence <\s>
<s> i found the old man's body in the moonlight hanging beneath the window of his chamber among the branches of a pine he could not have fallen there for all his limbs lay heaped 75 and effortless tis true there was no blood ... <\s>

<s> 95 lucretia her conduct throughout the scene is marked by extreme agitation ]: where was it found <\s>
<s> it should be orsino's hand <\s>
<s> it speaks of that strange horror which never yet found utterance but which made between that hapless child and her dead father a gulf of obscure hatred <\s>
<s> savella is it so <\s>
<s> 100 is it true lady that thy father did such outrages as to awaken in thee unfilial hate <\s>
<s> beatrice not hate twas more than hate this is most true yet wherefore question me <\s>
<s> savella there is a deed demanding question done 105 thou hast a secret which will answer not <\s>
<s> my lord your words are bold and rash <\s>
<s> savella i do arrest all present in the name of the pope's holiness <\s>
<s> you must to rome <\s>
<s> lucretia o not to rome <\s>
<s> indeed we are not guilty <\s>
<s> who dares talk of guilt <\s>
<s> my lord i am more innocent of parricide than is a child born fatherless ... dear mother your gentleness and patience are no shield for this keen judging world this two edged lie 115 which seems but is not <\s>
<s> will human laws rather will ye who are their ministers bar all access to retribution first and then when heaven doth interpose to do what ye neglect arming familiar things 120 to the redress of an unwonted crime make ye the victims who demanded it culprits <\s>
<s> tis ye are culprits <\s>
<s> that poor wretch who stands so pale and trembling and amazed if it be true he murdered cenci was 125 a sword in the right hand of justest god <\s>
<s> wherefore should i have wielded it <\s>
<s> unless the crimes which mortal tongue dare never name god therefore scruples to avenge <\s>
<s> savella you own that you desired his death <\s>
<s> beatrice it would have been 130 a crime no less than his if for one moment that fierce desire had faded in my heart <\s>
<s> tis true i did believe and hope and pray ay i even knew ... for god is wise and just that some strange sudden death hung over him <\s>
<s> 135 tis true that this did happen and most true there was no other rest for me on earth no other hope in heaven ... now what of this <\s>
<s> savella strange thoughts beget strange deeds and here are both i judge thee not <\s>
<s> beatrice and yet if you arrest me 140 you are the judge and executioner of that which is the life of life the breath of accusation kills an innocent name and leaves for lame acquittal the poor life which is a mask without it <\s>
<s> tis most false 145 that i am guilty of foul parricide although i must rejoice for justest cause that other hands have sent my father's soul to ask the mercy he denied to me <\s>
<s> now leave us free stain not a noble house 150 with vague surmises of rejected crime add to our sufferings and your own neglect no heavier sum let them have been enough leave us the wreck we have <\s>
<s> savella i dare not lady <\s>
<s> i pray that you prepare yourselves for rome 155 there the pope's further pleasure will be known <\s>
<s> lucretia o not to rome <\s>
<s> o take us not to rome <\s>
<s> beatrice why not to rome dear mother <\s>
<s> there as here our innocence is as an armed heel to trample accusation <\s>
<s> god is there 160 as here and with his shadow ever clothes the innocent the injured and the weak and such are we <\s>
<s> cheer up dear lady lean on me collect your wandering thoughts <\s>
<s> my lord as soon as you have taken some refreshment 165 and had all such examinations made upon the spot as may be necessary to the full understanding of this matter we shall be ready <\s>
<s> mother will you come <\s>
<s> they will bind us to the rack and wrest 170 self accusation from our agony <\s>
<s> will giacomo be there <\s>
<s> all present all confronted all demanding each from the other's countenance the thing which is in every heart <\s>
<s> 175 she faints and is borne out savella she faints an ill appearance this <\s>
<s> beatrice my lord she knows not yet the uses of the world <\s>
<s> she fears that power is as a beast which grasps and loosens not a snake whose look transmutes all things to guilt which is its nutriment <\s>
<s> 180 she cannot know how well the supine slaves of blind authority read the truth of things when written on a brow of guilelessness she sees not yet triumphant innocence stand at the judgement seat of mortal man 185 a judge and an accuser of the wrong which drags it there <\s>
<s> prepare yourself my lord our suite will join yours in the court below <\s>
<s> exeunt end of act 4 <\s>
<s> scene 5.1 an apartment in orsino's palace <\s>

<s> o that the vain remorse which must chastise crimes done had but as loud a voice to warn as its keen sting is mortal to avenge <\s>
